              SAMM Teknoloji has five different business segments: Telecommunication, Electrical heating, heat tracing,  Electric Contracting, Instrumentation, IT and IoT products.

SAMM Teknoloji is based in Gebze Organize Sanayi Bölgesi (GOSB) Gebze/Kocaeli - Turkiye

SAMM has been awarded R&amp;D Center Certificate in 2017


1-Telecommunication Department: We manufacture fiber optic cables, joint closures, distribution frames, MTP/MPO assemblies, patch cords and pigtails

2-Heating Department: SAMM is the leading company in Turkey for Electrical Heat Tracing  and electrical underfloor heating and snow and ice prevention.

3-IT Department: Developing SW/HW... And Raspberry Pi and Farnell official sales partner in Turkey to serve IT and IoT markets with a minimum cost to users.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">2024 yılı <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/turkishtime?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Turkishtime</a> tarafından hazırlanan “Ar-Ge 250, Türkiye’nin En Çok Ar-Ge Harcaması Yapan Şirketleri” araştırması sonuçlandı! 🎉

SAMM Teknoloji olarak, bu yıl da Ar-Ge’ye yaptığımız yatırımlar sayesinde Telekomünikasyon sektöründe 5. sıraya yükselmenin gururunu yaşıyoruz. 🚀

Bu başarı, Ar-Ge’ye olan bağlılığımızın bir sonucudur. Teknolojiye yön vermeye, geleceği birlikte inşa etmeye devam ediyoruz. 

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Farge250&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ArGe250</a> <a class="link"     <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Fiber Optic Sensing Association <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/fiber-optic-sensing-association?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Fiber Optic Sensing Association (FOSA)</a>, SAMM Teknoloji’nin Federated Learning ile fiber optik algılamaya getirdiği yenilikleri öne çıkardı. 🚀

Bu değerli paylaşım için FOSA’ya teşekkür eder, sektörümüzdeki gelişmelere katkı sunmaktan gurur duyarız. 

👉 Detaylar için: <a class="link" href="https://fotas.samm.com/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://fotas.samm.com/</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FfiberoptikalgAfTlama&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#FiberOptikAlgılama</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdas&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DAS</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FaltyapAfTgAeSvenliAfBi&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AltyapıGüvenliği</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsammteknoloji&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SAMMTeknoloji</a>

Fiber Optic Sensing Association (FOSA) has highlighted SAMM Teknoloji’s innovations in fiber optic sensing with Federated Learning. 🚀

We sincerely thank FOSA for this valuable recognition and are proud to contribute to advancements in our industry. 

👉 Read more: <a class="link" href="https://fotas.samm.com/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://fotas.samm.com/</a>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">Exciting new white paper from FOSA member SAMM Teknoloji explores how Federated Learning is transforming fiber optic sensing.
 
The paper introduces FOTAS with Federated Learning—a next-generation platform that combines Distributed Acoustic Sensing (DAS) with decentralized AI. This approach enables real-time, privacy-preserving monitoring across critical infrastructure like borders, pipelines, and industrial facilities.
 
Worth a quick read if you're interested in scalable, intelligent sensing systems that don’t compromise on data control.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">📢 Bu hafta haber bültenimizde Telgraftan CERN’in parçacık hızlandırıcılarına uzanan yolculuktan bahsettik.

Fiber optik kablolar, yalnızca interneti değil, modern bilimi de dönüştürdü. Bugün telekomünikasyondan veri merkezlerine, akıllı şehirlerden endüstriyel uygulamalara kadar pek çok alanda kritik rol oynuyor. Bu yazıda ışığın cam liflerdeki serüvenini ve geleceğimizi nasıl şekillendirdiğini keşfedeceksiniz. 

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ffiberoptik&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#FiberOptik</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FtelekomAeSnikasyon&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Telekomünikasyon</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2FendAeSstri&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Endüstri</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fbilimveteknoloji&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#BilimveTeknoloji</a>

📢 In this week's newsletter, we discussed the journey from the Telegraph to CERN's particle accelerators.

Fiber optic cables have transformed not only the internet but also modern science. Today, they play a critical role in many areas, from telecommunications and data centers to smart cities and industrial applications. In this article, you'll explore the journey of light through glass fibers and how it shapes our future.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Flightspeed&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text"     <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">İstanbul Atatürk Kültür Merkezi'nde  <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/t%C3%BCrk-telekom-ventures?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Türk Telekom Ventures</a>'ın ev sahipliğinde düzenlenen Global Value Growth etkinliği, girişimcilik ve yatırım ekosisteminin önde gelen VC ve CVC fonlarını, vizyoner iş liderlerini ve global yatırımcıları bir araya getirdi.

Girişimcilik, yatırım trendleri ve küresel ekonomik dinamikler üzerine yapılan tartışmaların öne çıktığı bu buluşmada, SAMM Teknoloji Yönetim Kurulu Başkanı <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/maksit/tr?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mustafa Aksit</a> de sahne alarak geleceğe yönelik vizyonunu ve stratejik bakış açısını paylaştı.

Bu seçkin etkinlikte, SAMM Teknoloji’nin küresel ekosisteme katkılarını paylaşmaktan gurur duyuyoruz. 

Held at Istanbul Atatürk Cultural Center, the Global Value Growth event, hosted by <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/t%C3%BCrk-telekom-ventures?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Türk Telekom Ventures</a> brought together leading VC and CVC funds, visionary business leaders, and global investors of the entrepreneurship and investment ecosystem.

The event featured discussions on entrepreneurship, investment trends, and global economic dynamics, where  <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/maksit/tr?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mustafa Aksit</a> , Chairman of the Board of SAMM Teknoloji, took the stage to share his forward-looking vision and strategic perspective.

We are proud to have shared SAMM Teknoloji’s contribution to the global ecosystem at this distinguished event.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">SAMM Teknoloji’nin Uşak’taki GES Projesi ile %100 Yeşil Enerji Ürettiğini Biliyor Muydunuz?

Güneş Enerji Santralimiz sayesinde tamamen çevre dostu enerji üretiyor, karbon ayak izimizi azaltıyoruz. 🌍🌱

Sürdürülebilir bir gelecek için çalışmaya devam ediyoruz.

Did you know that SAMM Teknoloji produces 100% Green Energy with its Solar Power Plant Project in Uşak?

Thanks to our Solar Power Plant, we generate completely eco-friendly energy and reduce our carbon footprint. 🌍🌱

We continue to work for a sustainable future.
